3. It looks like the hotel is being redone so half of the amenities were closed like the steak house and the theatre.
All in all it was extremely nice, a little inconvenient, but worth it.

This hotel is super clean! Our room got cleaned everyday and we got new towels and water. The room also comes with it's own swimming towels. The staff is very friendly, and during a heat wave we even got extra water. 
The pool is amazing! And the hotel is very beautiful, I understand why so many people go there to take photos. The hotel has afternoon tea, but we did not make use of it.

On the downside...Sanya bay does not have many choices to eat at. We did not book a room with breakfast included, because we did not want Cantonese breakfasts for 8 days. We thought we would be able to get breakfast at a nearby restaurant, but there where no nearby restaurants open for breakfast (there are McDonald's, KFC and Burger King close by if you like take out). The other places around the hotel are Chinese seafood restaurants and they only open around noon. The hotel has 2 restaurants, a Chinese and a Western. But they only serve dinner in the Chinese restaurant, and it's a set menu with 5 choices. The hotels also has no laundry service. It's says on C.trip that it has, but the only service is you walking to another hotel with your laundry or washing your clothes in the basin.

I have basically stayed in Sanya hotels. This time I wanted to choose a small and beautiful hotel. This hotel is completely in line with the price.

There is a problem with star-rated hotels. The interior is too big, the swimming pool and beach are far from the room, and there are too many people. Sanya Bay taxi, car rental, airport takeout is convenient, and it is also a plus for choosing this hotel.

The service of the hotel is very good. From Hu Tianxing, the concierge, to Sun Na, the lobby manager, everyone feels at home. They are attentive and attentive. They have principles and plans for many things, in order to satisfy the guests. Thank you!
